Within Customer Service we are not only responsible for the full order-to-cash process, but also for continuously improving the collaboration with our customers to build up a trustful relationship, improve processes and deliver best in class customer service.<\u002Fp> \n  <p>Do you dare to make an impact?<\u002Fp> \n  <h4 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b>YOUR ROLE<\u002Fb><\u002Fh4> \n  <ul>\n   <li>Be customers‘ counterpart for solving and negotiating any operational topic\u002Fissue related to orders (delays, incidents, returns, prices, invoices, etc…)<\u002Fli> \n   <li>Handle multiple sources of communication – phone, e-mail, <\u002Fli>\n   <li>Work cross functionally – Sales, Logistics, Demand Planning, 3PL, Marketing<\u002Fli> \n   <li>Ensure any solution(s) (Credit notes, Debit notes, Returns etc) are aligned and approved by relevant parties and while following Henkel Processes and guidelines<\u002Fli> \n   <li>Integration within a collaborative team with passion &amp;
